### Development Step 54: Identify 17th-Century Spectral Army Records, Locate Suffolk Supernatural Sites, Research Artist-Suffragette Locals

**Description**: Search for historical documents from the 17th century that record both a spectral army apparition in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain, focusing on identifying works like Joseph Glanvill's 'Saducismus Triumphatus' (1681) or similar collections of supernatural accounts. These compilations often documented multiple paranormal events across different locations. Once the specific document is identified, locate any Suffolk locations mentioned in connection with unusual supernatural events, then research notable individuals from that actual Suffolk place who were both artists and suffragettes.

**Use Cases**:
- Curatorial research for a Suffolk museum to identify 17th-century artist-suffragette figures from digitized archives and plan a themed exhibition
- Genealogy firm automating extraction from parish HTML and JSON records to help clients trace ancestors active in both art and women‚Äôs suffrage in Suffolk
- Digital humanities project mapping 17th-century paranormal accounts alongside local biographical data to build an interactive web atlas of supernatural events and notable residents
- University history department processing research files to cross-reference Glanvill‚Äôs ‚ÄòSaducismus Triumphatus‚Äô references with Suffolk artist-activists for a peer-reviewed journal article
- Cultural heritage NGO compiling an online database of female artist-suffragettes in rural Suffolk by scraping saved HTML research pages and structured JSON leads
- Local tourism board generating guided tour itineraries highlighting sites linked to prominent Suffolk suffragettes and artists, based on automated text analysis of archival materials
- Educational platform auto-generating lesson modules on East Anglian women‚Äôs history by extracting and validating names from digitized Suffolk research files
- Arts funding body analyzing extracted individual profiles to prioritize grants for preserving suffrage movement art heritage sites in Suffolk

import os
import json
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

print('=== EXTRACTING SPECIFIC ARTIST/SUFFRAGETTE NAMES FROM SUFFOLK RESEARCH FILES ===')
print('Previous search identified 5 promising Suffolk locations with artist/suffragette connections')
print('Now extracting specific individual names from the saved HTML research files\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# First, let's inspect the comprehensive research file to understand its structure
research_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'comprehensive_historical_suffolk_research.json')

print('=== PHASE 1: INSPECTING SAVED RESEARCH DATA ===')
print('=' * 70)

if os.path.exists(research_file):
print(f'Found research file: {research_file}')

try:
with open(research_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
research_data = json.load(f)

print('Research file structure:')
for key in research_data.keys():
if isinstance(research_data[key], list):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(research_data[key])} items')
elif isinstance(research_data[key], dict):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(research_data[key])} keys')
else:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {type(research_data[key]).__name__}')

# Examine the artist_suffragette_leads structure
if 'artist_suffragette_leads' in research_data:
print(f'\nArtist/Suffragette leads found: {len(research_data["artist_suffragette_leads"])}')

for i, lead in enumerate(research_data['artist_suffragette_leads'], 1):
print(f' {i}. {lead["location"]} - Promising: {lead.get("promising", False)}')
if 'artist_search' in lead and 'file' in lead['artist_search']:
print(f' Artist file: {lead["artist_search"]["file"]}')
if 'suffragette_search' in lead and 'file' in lead['suffragette_search']:
print(f' Suffragette file: {lead["suffragette_search"]["file"]}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error reading research file: {str(e)}')
else:
print(f'Research file not found: {research_file}')
print('Checking for alternative research files...')

# Look for any JSON files in workspace
json_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')]
print(f'Found {len(json_files)} JSON files:')
for f in json_files:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {f}')

print('\n=== PHASE 2: EXAMINING HTML RESEARCH FILES FOR SPECIFIC NAMES ===')
print('=' * 80)

# Look for HTML files related to Suffolk locations
html_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.html') and any(location in f.lower() for location in ['aldeburgh', 'bury', 'lavenham', 'melford', 'woodbridge'])]

print(f'Found {len(html_files)} Suffolk location HTML files:')
for f in html_files:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {f}')

# Initialize results storage
name_extraction_results = {
'timestamp': '2024-12-19',
'objective': 'Extract specific artist and suffragette names from Suffolk location research',
'locations_analyzed': [],
'individuals_found': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

# Process each HTML file to extract names
for html_file in html_files:
print(f'\n--- Analyzing {html_file} ---')

# Determine location from filename
location = 'Unknown'
if 'aldeburgh' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Aldeburgh'
elif 'bury' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Bury St Edmunds'
elif 'lavenham' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Lavenham'
elif 'melford' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Long Melford'
elif 'woodbridge' in html_file.lower():
location = 'Woodbridge'

# Determine if this is artist or suffragette search
search_type = 'artist' if 'artist' in html_file.lower() else 'suffragette'

print(f'Location: {location}, Search type: {search_type}')

try:
html_filepath = os.path.join('workspace', html_file)
with open(html_filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
html_content = f.read()

print(f'File size: {len(html_content):,} characters')

# Parse HTML content
soup = BeautifulSoup(html_content, 'html.parser')

# Extract text content
page_text = soup.get_text()

# Look for potential names using various patterns
potential_names = set()

# Pattern 1: Names in titles or headings
for heading in soup.find_all(['h1', 'h2', 'h3', 'h4', 'title']):
heading_text = heading.get_text().strip()
# Look for capitalized words that might be names
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', heading_text)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Pattern 2: Names in context with artist/suffragette keywords
text_lines = page_text.split('\n')
for line in text_lines:
line = line.strip()
if len(line) > 20 and len(line) < 200: # Reasonable line length
# Look for lines containing relevant keywords
if search_type == 'artist':
if any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['artist', 'painter', 'sculptor', 'born', 'lived']):
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', line)
potential_names.update(name_matches)
else: # suffragette
if any(keyword in line.lower() for keyword in ['suffragette', 'suffrage', 'women', 'rights', 'activist']):
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', line)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Pattern 3: Names in link text or descriptions
for link in soup.find_all('a'):
link_text = link.get_text().strip()
if len(link_text) > 5 and len(link_text) < 100:
name_matches = re.findall(r'\b[A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+\b', link_text)
potential_names.update(name_matches)

# Filter out common false positives
filtered_names = set()
false_positives = {'New York', 'United States', 'Great Britain', 'Long Island', 'New England',
'World War', 'First World', 'Second World', 'High School', 'Art Gallery',
'Art Museum', 'Women Rights', 'Human Rights', 'Civil Rights', 'Royal Academy'}

for name in potential_names:
if name not in false_positives and len(name.split()) == 2:
# Additional filtering for likely person names
first_name, last_name = name.split()
if len(first_name) > 2 and len(last_name) > 2:
filtered_names.add(name)

print(f'Found {len(filtered_names)} potential names: {list(filtered_names)[:5]}...')

# Store results
location_analysis = {
'location': location,
'search_type': search_type,
'html_file': html_file,
'potential_names': list(filtered_names),
'name_count': len(filtered_names)
}

name_extraction_results['locations_analyzed'].append(location_analysis)

# Add individual names to master list
for name in filtered_names:
individual_entry = {
'name': name,
'location': location,
'type': search_type,
'source_file': html_file
}
name_extraction_results['individuals_found'].append(individual_entry)

# Show most promising findings
if len(filtered_names) > 0:
print(f'üéØ NAMES FOUND in {location} ({search_type}):'):
for name in list(filtered_names)[:3]: # Show top 3
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name}')
else:
print(f'‚ùå No clear names found in {location} ({search_type})')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error processing {html_file}: {str(e)}')

print('\n=== PHASE 3: ANALYZING EXTRACTED NAMES AND IDENTIFYING MOST PROMISING CANDIDATES ===')
print('=' * 90)

total_individuals = len(name_extraction_results['individuals_found'])
print(f'Total individuals extracted: {total_individuals}')

if total_individuals > 0:
# Group by location
by_location = {}
by_type = {'artist': [], 'suffragette': []}

for individual in name_extraction_results['individuals_found']:
location = individual['location']
if location not in by_location:
by_location[location] = []
by_location[location].append(individual)

by_type[individual['type']].append(individual)

print(f'\nüìç INDIVIDUALS BY LOCATION:')
for location, individuals in by_location.items():
print(f' {location}: {len(individuals)} individuals')
artists = [i for i in individuals if i['type'] == 'artist']
suffragettes = [i for i in individuals if i['type'] == 'suffragette']
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Artists: {len(artists)}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Suffragettes: {len(suffragettes)}')

# Show sample names
if artists:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Sample artists: {", ".join([a["name"] for a in artists[:2]])}')
if suffragettes:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Sample suffragettes: {", ".join([s["name"] for s in suffragettes[:2]])}')

print(f'\nüë• INDIVIDUALS BY TYPE:')
print(f' Artists: {len(by_type["artist"])}')
print(f' Suffragettes: {len(by_type["suffragette"])}')

# Identify individuals who appear in both categories (most promising)
artist_names = set([i['name'] for i in by_type['artist']])
suffragette_names = set([i['name'] for i in by_type['suffragette']])

dual_individuals = artist_names.intersection(suffragette_names)

if dual_individuals:
print(f'\nüéØ INDIVIDUALS WHO ARE BOTH ARTISTS AND SUFFRAGETTES ({len(dual_individuals)}):'):
for name in dual_individuals:
# Find their locations
locations = set()
for individual in name_extraction_results['individuals_found']:
if individual['name'] == name:
locations.add(individual['location'])
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(locations)})')
else:
print('\n‚ùå No individuals found who are both artists and suffragettes')
print('Showing top candidates from each category:')

if by_type['artist']:
print('\nüé® TOP ARTISTS:')
unique_artists = list(set([i['name'] for i in by_type['artist']]))
for name in unique_artists[:5]:
locations = [i['location'] for i in by_type['artist'] if i['name'] == name]
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(set(locations))})')

if by_type['suffragette']:
print('\nüó≥Ô∏è TOP SUFFRAGETTES:')
unique_suffragettes = list(set([i['name'] for i in by_type['suffragette']]))
for name in unique_suffragettes[:5]:
locations = [i['location'] for i in by_type['suffragette'] if i['name'] == name]
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {name} (from {', '.join(set(locations))})')
else:
print('‚ùå No individual names were successfully extracted from the research files')
print('This could indicate:')
print(' ‚Ä¢ The HTML files may not contain detailed biographical information')
print(' ‚Ä¢ The search results may be too general or not focused on individuals')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Additional targeted searches may be needed for specific people')

# Save extraction results
extraction_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'suffolk_individuals_extracted.json')

name_extraction_results['analysis_summary'] = {
'total_individuals': total_individuals,
'locations_with_findings': len([loc for loc in name_extraction_results['locations_analyzed'] if loc['name_count'] > 0]),
'artists_found': len([i for i in name_extraction_results['individuals_found'] if i['type'] == 'artist']),
'suffragettes_found': len([i for i in name_extraction_results['individuals_found'] if i['type'] == 'suffragette']),
'dual_individuals': len(dual_individuals) if total_individuals > 0 else 0
}

with open(extraction_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(name_extraction_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ NAME EXTRACTION RESULTS SAVED TO: {extraction_file}')

print('\n=== PHASE 4: RECOMMENDATIONS FOR COMPLETING THE RESEARCH ===')
print('=' * 80)

if total_individuals > 0:
print('‚úÖ SUCCESS: Individual names have been extracted from Suffolk location research')
print('\nüéØ NEXT STEPS TO COMPLETE THE RESEARCH:')
print('1. üìö Conduct detailed biographical research on the extracted individuals')
print('2. ‚úÖ Verify their connections to both art and suffrage movements')
print('3. üìç Confirm their association with the identified Suffolk locations')
print('4. üîç Cross-reference with historical records and databases')

if dual_individuals:
print(f'5. üéØ Priority focus on dual individuals: {", ".join(list(dual_individuals)[:3])}')
else:
print('5. üîÑ Research connections between top artists and suffragettes from same locations')
else:
print('‚ö†Ô∏è ALTERNATIVE APPROACH NEEDED:')
print('1. üîç Conduct more targeted searches for specific Suffolk artists')
print('2. üìö Search historical databases and archives directly')
print('3. üèõÔ∏è Check local Suffolk historical society records')
print('4. üìñ Examine biographical dictionaries of British artists and suffragettes')

print('\nüìä FINAL EXTRACTION STATISTICS:')
for key, value in name_extraction_results['analysis_summary'].items():
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key.replace("_", " ").title()}: {value}')

print('\n=== SUFFOLK ARTIST/SUFFRAGETTE NAME EXTRACTION COMPLETE ===')
```

### Development Step 48: Identify 17th-Century Supernatural Accounts (Spectral Army), Find Suffolk Sites, Research Artist-Suffragettes

**Description**: Search for historical documents from the 17th century that record both a spectral army apparition in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain, focusing on identifying works like Joseph Glanvill's 'Saducismus Triumphatus' (1681) or similar collections of supernatural accounts. These compilations often documented multiple paranormal events across different locations. Once the specific document is identified, locate any Suffolk locations mentioned in connection with unusual supernatural events, then research notable individuals from that actual Suffolk place who were both artists and suffragettes.

**Use Cases**:
- Academic historical research and digital humanities mapping of 17th-century supernatural accounts across Britain and Ireland to study cultural beliefs and religious dissent
- Museum exhibition curation using references to paranormal events in Suffolk to design immersive local-history displays that feature suffragette-artists from Ipswich and Framlingham
- Genealogical investigation tracing family links to spectral army apparitions in 17th-century Ireland and later suffragette-artist ancestors in Suffolk villages
- Cultural tourism development by creating guided ghost-tour itineraries in Lowestoft and Bury St Edmunds, highlighting folklore sites and their connections to women artists and suffragettes
- Educational curriculum design integrating primary sources like Saducismus Triumphatus and Suffolk supernatural events into secondary-school modules on early modern witchcraft and the women‚Äôs rights movement
- Digital archive management automating metadata extraction for 17th-century supernatural compilations, tagging documents by location and associated suffrage-era figures for online repositories
- Feminist art history analysis researching how paranormal folklore documented in Suffolk influenced the creative practices of local suffragette painters and sculptors
- Heritage preservation planning using compiled records of spectral sightings and suffragette-artist biographies to nominate Woodbridge and Sudbury landmarks for protected status

```
import os
import requests
import json
import time
from urllib.parse import quote_plus
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
from collections import Counter

print('=== SEARCH FOR 17TH CENTURY SUPERNATURAL DOCUMENTS ===')
print('Objective: Find historical documents recording spectral army apparitions in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain')
print('Focus: Joseph Glanvill\'s "Saducismus Triumphatus" (1681) and similar collections\n')

# Ensure workspace directory exists
os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True)

# Initialize comprehensive search results storage
search_results = {
'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'),
'objective': 'Find 17th century documents with spectral army apparitions in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain',
'target_works': ['Saducismus Triumphatus', 'Joseph Glanvill', '17th century supernatural compilations'],
'search_queries': [],
'findings': [],
'document_candidates': [],
'suffolk_connections': [],
'analysis_summary': {}
}

print('TARGET DOCUMENT CHARACTERISTICS:')
print('‚Ä¢ Time period: 17th century (1600-1699)')
print('‚Ä¢ Content: Spectral army apparitions in Ireland')
print('‚Ä¢ Content: Supernatural events in Britain')
print('‚Ä¢ Type: Historical compilations/collections')
print('‚Ä¢ Key work: Joseph Glanvill\'s "Saducismus Triumphatus" (1681)')
print('‚Ä¢ Goal: Identify Suffolk locations with supernatural events')
print('‚Ä¢ Final goal: Find artists/suffragettes from those Suffolk locations\n')

# Define targeted search queries
search_queries = [
'"Saducismus Triumphatus" Joseph Glanvill 1681 spectral army Ireland',
'Joseph Glanvill supernatural events Britain Ireland 17th century',
'"spectral army" apparition Ireland 17th century historical document',
'17th century supernatural compilation Britain Ireland paranormal accounts',
'Glanvill witchcraft supernatural events Suffolk Britain 1681',
'"Saducismus Triumphatus" Suffolk supernatural events locations',
'17th century ghost stories Ireland Britain historical records',
'Joseph Glanvill paranormal collection Ireland spectral phenomena'
]

print(f'Executing {len(search_queries)} targeted searches:')
for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f' {i}. {query}')

# Headers for web requests
headers = {
'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36',
'Accept': 'text/html,application/xhtml+xml,application/xml;q=0.9,*/*;q=0.8',
'Accept-Language': 'en-US,en;q=0.9',
'Connection': 'keep-alive'
}

print('\n=== PHASE 1: TARGETED SEARCHES FOR GLANVILL AND 17TH CENTURY SUPERNATURAL WORKS ===')
print('=' * 80)

for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):
print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}')
print('-' * 70)

try:
# Construct Google search URL
google_url = f'https://www.google.com/search?q={quote_plus(query)}'
print(f'URL: {google_url}')

response = requests.get(google_url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
print(f'Status: {response.status_code}')

if response.status_code == 200:
# Save HTML for reference
filename = f'search_{i}_{query[:50].replace(" ", "_").replace("\'\'", "").replace('"', "")}.html'
filepath = os.path.join('workspace', filename)

with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
f.write(response.text)

print(f'Saved: {filepath}')

# Parse results
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Extract text content for analysis
page_text = soup.get_text().lower()

# Look for key terms and calculate relevance
key_terms = {
'glanvill': 5,
'saducismus': 5,
'triumphatus': 5,
'1681': 4,
'spectral': 4,
'army': 3,
'apparition': 4,
'ireland': 4,
'supernatural': 3,
'britain': 3,
'suffolk': 5,
'17th': 3,
'century': 2,
'witchcraft': 3,
'paranormal': 3,
'ghost': 2,
'compilation': 3,
'collection': 2
}

found_terms = []
relevance_score = 0

for term, weight in key_terms.items():
if term in page_text:
found_terms.append(term)
relevance_score += weight

print(f'Relevance score: {relevance_score}')
print(f'Found terms: {", ".join(found_terms[:10])}')

# Look for Suffolk mentions specifically
suffolk_mentions = []
if 'suffolk' in page_text:
print('‚úì Found Suffolk - extracting context...')

# Find sentences containing Suffolk
sentences = page_text.split('.')
for sentence in sentences:
if 'suffolk' in sentence and len(sentence.strip()) > 10:
suffolk_mentions.append(sentence.strip()[:200])
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Suffolk context: {sentence.strip()[:150]}...')

search_results['suffolk_connections'].extend(suffolk_mentions)

# Look for specific document titles and authors
document_indicators = []
if 'saducismus triumphatus' in page_text:
document_indicators.append('Saducismus Triumphatus confirmed')
print('üéØ SADUCISMUS TRIUMPHATUS FOUND!')

if 'joseph glanvill' in page_text:
document_indicators.append('Joseph Glanvill confirmed')
print('üéØ JOSEPH GLANVILL CONFIRMED!')

if 'spectral army' in page_text:
document_indicators.append('Spectral army reference found')
print('üëª SPECTRAL ARMY REFERENCE FOUND!')

# Store finding
finding = {
'query': query,
'relevance_score': relevance_score,
'found_terms': found_terms,
'has_suffolk': 'suffolk' in page_text,
'suffolk_contexts': suffolk_mentions,
'document_indicators': document_indicators,
'html_file': filepath
}

search_results['findings'].append(finding)
search_results['search_queries'].append(query)

# If high relevance, mark as document candidate
if relevance_score >= 15 or len(document_indicators) >= 2:
print('üìö HIGH RELEVANCE - Adding to document candidates...')
search_results['document_candidates'].append(finding)

# Extract more detailed information
text_snippets = []
sentences = page_text.split('.')

for sentence in sentences:
if any(term in sentence for term in ['glanvill', 'saducismus', 'spectral', 'supernatural']):
if len(sentence.strip()) > 20 and len(sentence.strip()) < 300:
text_snippets.append(sentence.strip())

if text_snippets:
print('Key text snippets found:')
for j, snippet in enumerate(text_snippets[:3], 1):
print(f' {j}. {snippet[:200]}...')

finding['key_snippets'] = text_snippets[:5]

else:
print(f'Failed with status {response.status_code}')

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error: {str(e)}')

time.sleep(3) # Rate limiting

print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR DOCUMENT IDENTIFICATION')
print('=' * 80)

total_findings = len(search_results['findings'])
print(f'Total search results: {total_findings}')
print(f'Document candidates: {len(search_results["document_candidates"])}')
print(f'Suffolk connections found: {len(search_results["suffolk_connections"])}')

if search_results['findings']:
# Sort by relevance score
search_results['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True)

print('\nüìä RELEVANCE ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 40)

high_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 15]
moderate_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 8 <= f['relevance_score'] < 15]

print(f'High relevance results (15+ points): {len(high_relevance)}')
print(f'Moderate relevance results (8-14 points): {len(moderate_relevance)}')

if high_relevance:
print('\nüéØ HIGH RELEVANCE FINDINGS:')
for i, finding in enumerate(high_relevance, 1):
print(f'\n{i}. Query: {finding["query"]}')
print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}')
print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:8])}')
print(f' Has Suffolk: {finding["has_suffolk"]}')
print(f' Document indicators: {", ".join(finding["document_indicators"])}')
if finding.get('key_snippets'):
print(f' Key snippet: {finding["key_snippets"][0][:150]}...')

# Analyze all terms found
all_terms = []
for finding in search_results['findings']:
all_terms.extend(finding['found_terms'])

term_counts = Counter(all_terms)
print('\nüìà TERM FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 30)
for term, count in term_counts.most_common(10):
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {term}: {count} mentions')

# Compile evidence for document identification
evidence_strength = {
'glanvill_confirmed': any('glanvill' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']),
'saducismus_confirmed': any('saducismus' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']),
'spectral_army_found': any('spectral' in f['found_terms'] and 'army' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']),
'ireland_connection': any('ireland' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']),
'suffolk_locations': any(f['has_suffolk'] for f in search_results['findings']),
'17th_century_confirmed': any('17th' in f['found_terms'] or '1681' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings'])
}

print('\nüîç EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:')
print('-' * 30)
for evidence, confirmed in evidence_strength.items():
status = '‚úÖ' if confirmed else '‚ùå'
print(f'{status} {evidence.replace("_", " ").title()}: {confirmed}')

search_results['analysis_summary']['evidence_strength'] = evidence_strength

# Calculate overall confidence
confirmed_count = sum(evidence_strength.values())
confidence_percentage = (confirmed_count / len(evidence_strength)) * 100

print(f'\nüìà OVERALL CONFIDENCE: {confidence_percentage:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(evidence_strength)} criteria met)')
search_results['analysis_summary']['confidence_percentage'] = confidence_percentage

else:
print('‚ùå No search results collected')

# Analyze Suffolk connections specifically
if search_results['suffolk_connections']:
print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('PHASE 3: ANALYZING SUFFOLK CONNECTIONS')
print('=' * 80)

print(f'Found {len(search_results["suffolk_connections"])} Suffolk references:')

unique_suffolk_contexts = list(set(search_results['suffolk_connections']))
for i, context in enumerate(unique_suffolk_contexts[:5], 1):
print(f'\n{i}. {context[:250]}...')

# Look for specific Suffolk place names in the contexts
suffolk_places = [
'ipswich', 'bury st edmunds', 'lowestoft', 'felixstowe', 'sudbury',
'haverhill', 'newmarket', 'stowmarket', 'woodbridge', 'aldeburgh',
'beccles', 'eye', 'framlingham', 'leiston', 'mildenhall', 'saxmundham'
]

found_places = []
for context in search_results['suffolk_connections']:
context_lower = context.lower()
for place in suffolk_places:
if place in context_lower and place not in found_places:
found_places.append(place)
print(f'üéØ SUFFOLK PLACE IDENTIFIED: {place.title()}')

search_results['analysis_summary']['suffolk_places_found'] = found_places

# Save comprehensive results
results_file = os.path.join('workspace', '17th_century_supernatural_documents_search.json')
with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)

print(f'\nüíæ COMPREHENSIVE RESULTS SAVED TO: {results_file}')

# Final conclusions
print('\n' + '=' * 80)
print('FINAL CONCLUSIONS - PHASE 1 COMPLETE')
print('=' * 80)

print('üìñ DOCUMENT IDENTIFICATION STATUS:')
if search_results.get('analysis_summary', {}).get('confidence_percentage', 0) >= 60:
print('‚úÖ PRIMARY DOCUMENT LIKELY IDENTIFIED:')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Work: "Saducismus Triumphatus" by Joseph Glanvill (1681)')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Content: Collection of supernatural accounts from Britain and Ireland')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Includes: Spectral army apparitions and paranormal events')
else:
print('‚ùì DOCUMENT IDENTIFICATION NEEDS VERIFICATION')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Review search results for alternative 17th century supernatural compilations')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Consider other authors like Richard Baxter, Increase Mather, or Cotton Mather')

if search_results.get('analysis_summary', {}).get('suffolk_places_found'):
print('\nüéØ SUFFOLK LOCATIONS IDENTIFIED:')
for place in search_results['analysis_summary']['suffolk_places_found']:
print(f' ‚Ä¢ {place.title()}')
else:
print('\n‚ùì SUFFOLK LOCATIONS NEED FURTHER INVESTIGATION')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Review saved HTML files for specific Suffolk place names')
print(' ‚Ä¢ Conduct targeted searches for Suffolk supernatural events')

print('\nüìã NEXT STEPS:')
print('1. üîç Review high-relevance search results for specific Suffolk locations')
print('2. üìö Investigate "Saducismus Triumphatus" content for Suffolk supernatural events')
print('3. üèõÔ∏è Once Suffolk location identified, search for artists and suffragettes from that place')
print('4. üìÑ Examine saved HTML files for additional context and details')

print('\nüìä SEARCH SUMMARY:')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Queries executed: {len(search_results["search_queries"])}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Results collected: {len(search_results["findings"])}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Document candidates: {len(search_results["document_candidates"])}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ Suffolk connections: {len(search_results["suffolk_connections"])}')
print(f' ‚Ä¢ HTML files saved: {len([f for f in search_results["findings"] if f.get("html_file")])}')

print('\n=== 17TH CENTURY SUPERNATURAL DOCUMENTS SEARCH - PHASE 1 COMPLETE ===')
```

### Development Step 59: Identify 17th-Century British-Irish Supernatural Compendium & Suffolk Suffragette-Artists

**Description**: Search for historical documents from the 17th century that record both a spectral army apparition in Ireland and supernatural events in Britain, focusing on identifying works like Joseph Glanvill's 'Saducismus Triumphatus' (1681) or similar collections of supernatural accounts. These compilations often documented multiple paranormal events across different locations. Once the specific document is identified, locate any Suffolk locations mentioned in connection with unusual supernatural events, then research notable individuals from that actual Suffolk place who were both artists and suffragettes.

**Use Cases**:
- Digital humanities project automating cross-referencing 17th-century supernatural manuscripts with suffragette archives to build an interactive map of Suffolk‚Äôs cultural heritage
- Museum exhibition development extracting folklore site data and artist-suffragette biographies for a multimedia display on women‚Äôs activism in haunted locales
- Heritage tourism initiative mapping spectral event records and suffrage movement figures into guided walking tours of Suffolk‚Äôs supernatural landmarks
- Academic thesis research leveraging automated analysis of Saducismus Triumphatus texts and suffrage records to study the impact of paranormal belief on female artists
- Genealogy service cross-validating ancestral records with paranormal event logs and suffrage membership to trace family connections to haunted Suffolk sites
- Documentary production sourcing primary 17th-century apparition accounts and suffragette artist profiles to narrate a film on paranormal influences in women's rights history
- Digital archive platform implementing NLP and web-scraping pipelines to catalog apparition narratives and suffragette metadata for advanced historical research
- Local council heritage app integrating ghost stories and suffrage activism itineraries into a mobile guide for community history engagement

```
import os

]

if 'final_answer' in data:

except Exception as e:
print(f'Error reading {filename}: {str(e)}')
else:
print(f'File not found: {filename}')

import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from ddgs import DDGS print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE SOUTH LONDON ===') print('Objective: Identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its Victorian-era development history') print('Focus: Temperance hall transformation, rotating stage (1935), WWII damage, Burnley relocation') print('Goal: Find founder of organization that developed Surrey Lodge and their birth year\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize comprehensive search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Surrey Lodge South London - Victorian development to modern history', 'search_focus': { 'location': 'Surrey Lodge, South London', 'historical_periods': ['Victorian era', '1935 rotating stage', 'WWII bomb damage'], 'key_events': ['temperance hall transformation', 'first rotating stage UK', 'company relocation to Burnley'], 'ultimate_goal': 'Find founder birth year' }, 'search_queries': [], 'findings': [], 'venue_candidates': [], 'historical_timeline': {}, 'founder_leads': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print('TARGET INFORMATION TO LOCATE:') print('‚Ä¢ Location: Surrey Lodge in South London') print('‚Ä¢ Victorian-era development history') print('‚Ä¢ Transformation into temperance hall') print('‚Ä¢ Installation of UK\'s first rotating stage (1935)') print('‚Ä¢ World War II bomb damage') print('‚Ä¢ Associated company relocation to Burnley') print('‚Ä¢ Founder of original developing organization') print('‚Ä¢ Founder\'s birth year\n') # Define comprehensive search queries search_queries = [ '"Surrey Lodge" South London Victorian temperance hall history', 'Surrey Lodge London rotating stage 1935 first UK', '"Surrey Lodge" South London World War II bomb damage', 'Surrey Lodge temperance hall company Burnley relocation', 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian development founder', '"Surrey Lodge" London theatre rotating stage history', 'South London Surrey Lodge temperance movement Victorian', 'Surrey Lodge founder birth year Victorian temperance organization', '"Surrey Lodge" London WWII damage reconstruction history', 'temperance hall Surrey Lodge South London rotating stage 1935' ] print(f'Executing {len(search_queries)} comprehensive searches:\n') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') print('\n=== PHASE 1: SYSTEMATIC WEB SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE ===') print('=' * 70) # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Perform search with multiple backends results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-gb" # UK region for better local results ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') # Process each result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title[:100]}...') print(f' URL: {url}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...') # Analyze relevance relevance_score = 0 key_terms = { 'surrey lodge': 5, 'south london': 4, 'temperance': 4, 'rotating stage': 5, '1935': 4, 'victorian': 3, 'bomb damage': 4, 'burnley': 4, 'founder': 4, 'theatre': 3, 'hall': 2, 'wwii': 3, 'world war': 3 } found_terms = [] combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() for term, weight in key_terms.items(): if term in combined_text: found_terms.append(term) relevance_score += weight print(f' Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f' Found terms: {", ".join(found_terms[:5])}') # Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'search_index': i, 'result_index': j } search_results['findings'].append(result_data) # Mark high-relevance results as venue candidates if relevance_score >= 8: print(f' üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE - Adding to venue candidates') search_results['venue_candidates'].append(result_data) # Try to extract the webpage content for detailed analysis try: print(f' üìÑ Attempting to fetch webpage content...') headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } page_response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=10) if page_response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(page_response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract text content page_text = soup.get_text() # Save webpage content safe_filename = f'surrey_lodge_search_{i}_{j}_{title[:30].replace(" ", "_").replace("/", "_")}.html' safe_filename = re.sub(r'[^\w\-_\.]', '_', safe_filename) filepath = os.path.join('workspace', safe_filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(page_response.text) print(f' üíæ Saved webpage: {safe_filename}') result_data['saved_file'] = safe_filename # Look for specific historical details in the content historical_indicators = { 'rotating stage': 'rotating stage installation', '1935': 'year 1935 mentioned', 'temperance hall': 'temperance hall reference', 'victorian': 'victorian era connection', 'bomb damage': 'wwii bomb damage', 'burnley': 'burnley relocation', 'founder': 'founder information' } page_text_lower = page_text.lower() historical_findings = [] for indicator, description in historical_indicators.items(): if indicator in page_text_lower: historical_findings.append(description) print(f' ‚úì Found: {description}') result_data['historical_findings'] = historical_findings # Look for birth years and founder names birth_year_pattern = r'\b(18\d{2}|19\d{2})\b' birth_years = re.findall(birth_year_pattern, page_text) if birth_years: print(f' üìÖ Potential birth years found: {", ".join(set(birth_years)[:5])}') result_data['potential_birth_years'] = list(set(birth_years)) # Look for founder names founder_patterns = [ r'founder[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'founded by[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'established by[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)' ] potential_founders = [] for pattern in founder_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) potential_founders.extend(matches) if potential_founders: unique_founders = list(set(potential_founders)) print(f' üë§ Potential founders: {", ".join(unique_founders[:3])}') result_data['potential_founders'] = unique_founders # Add to founder leads for founder in unique_founders: search_results['founder_leads'].append({ 'name': founder, 'source_url': url, 'source_query': query, 'context': 'Surrey Lodge research' }) else: print(f' ‚ùå Failed to fetch webpage (status: {page_response.status_code})') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ö†Ô∏è Error fetching webpage: {str(e)}') else: print('‚ùå No results found for this query') search_results['search_queries'].append(query) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR SURREY LODGE IDENTIFICATION') print('=' * 80) total_findings = len(search_results['findings']) print(f'Total search results collected: {total_findings}') print(f'High-relevance venue candidates: {len(search_results["venue_candidates"])}') print(f'Potential founder leads: {len(search_results["founder_leads"])}') if search_results['findings']: # Sort by relevance score search_results['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüìä RELEVANCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) high_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 8] moderate_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 4 <= f['relevance_score'] < 8] print(f'High relevance results (8+ points): {len(high_relevance)}') print(f'Moderate relevance results (4-7 points): {len(moderate_relevance)}') if high_relevance: print('\nüéØ TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:') for i, finding in enumerate(high_relevance[:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Title: {finding["title"][:80]}...') print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:6])}') if finding.get('historical_findings'): print(f' Historical: {", ".join(finding["historical_findings"][:3])}') if finding.get('potential_founders'): print(f' Founders: {", ".join(finding["potential_founders"][:2])}') if finding.get('potential_birth_years'): print(f' Birth years: {", ".join(finding["potential_birth_years"][:3])}') # Analyze founder leads if search_results['founder_leads']: print('\nüë§ FOUNDER LEADS ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 30) founder_names = [lead['name'] for lead in search_results['founder_leads']] unique_founders = list(set(founder_names)) print(f'Unique potential founders identified: {len(unique_founders)}') for founder in unique_founders[:5]: count = founder_names.count(founder) print(f' ‚Ä¢ {founder} (mentioned {count} time{"s" if count > 1 else ""})') # Create historical timeline from findings timeline_events = [] for finding in search_results['findings']: if finding.get('historical_findings'): for event in finding['historical_findings']: timeline_events.append({ 'event': event, 'source': finding['title'], 'url': finding['url'] }) if timeline_events: print('\nüìÖ HISTORICAL TIMELINE EVENTS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 45) unique_events = [] for event in timeline_events: if event['event'] not in [e['event'] for e in unique_events]: unique_events.append(event) for event in unique_events[:8]: import os import requests import json import time from urllib.parse import quote_plus from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from ddgs import DDGS print('=== COMPREHENSIVE SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE SOUTH LONDON ===') print('Objective: Identify Surrey Lodge in South London and trace its Victorian-era development history') print('Focus: Temperance hall transformation, rotating stage (1935), WWII damage, Burnley relocation') print('Goal: Find founder of organization that developed Surrey Lodge and their birth year\n') # Ensure workspace directory exists os.makedirs('workspace', exist_ok=True) # Initialize comprehensive search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Surrey Lodge South London - Victorian development to modern history', 'search_focus': { 'location': 'Surrey Lodge, South London', 'historical_periods': ['Victorian era', '1935 rotating stage', 'WWII bomb damage'], 'key_events': ['temperance hall transformation', 'first rotating stage UK', 'company relocation to Burnley'], 'ultimate_goal': 'Find founder birth year' }, 'search_queries': [], 'findings': [], 'venue_candidates': [], 'historical_timeline': {}, 'founder_leads': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } print('TARGET INFORMATION TO LOCATE:') print('‚Ä¢ Location: Surrey Lodge in South London') print('‚Ä¢ Victorian-era development history') print('‚Ä¢ Transformation into temperance hall') print('‚Ä¢ Installation of UK\'s first rotating stage (1935)') print('‚Ä¢ World War II bomb damage') print('‚Ä¢ Associated company relocation to Burnley') print('‚Ä¢ Founder of original developing organization') print('‚Ä¢ Founder\'s birth year\n') # Define comprehensive search queries search_queries = [ '"Surrey Lodge" South London Victorian temperance hall history', 'Surrey Lodge London rotating stage 1935 first UK', '"Surrey Lodge" South London World War II bomb damage', 'Surrey Lodge temperance hall company Burnley relocation', 'Surrey Lodge South London Victorian development founder', '"Surrey Lodge" London theatre rotating stage history', 'South London Surrey Lodge temperance movement Victorian', 'Surrey Lodge founder birth year Victorian temperance organization', '"Surrey Lodge" London WWII damage reconstruction history', 'temperance hall Surrey Lodge South London rotating stage 1935' ] print(f'Executing {len(search_queries)} comprehensive searches:\n') for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') print('\n=== PHASE 1: SYSTEMATIC WEB SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE ===') print('=' * 70) # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) for i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(search_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Perform search with multiple backends results = searcher.text( query, max_results=10, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing", "yahoo"], safesearch="off", region="en-gb" # UK region for better local results ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') # Process each result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title[:100]}...') print(f' URL: {url}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...') # Analyze relevance relevance_score = 0 key_terms = { 'surrey lodge': 5, 'south london': 4, 'temperance': 4, 'rotating stage': 5, '1935': 4, 'victorian': 3, 'bomb damage': 4, 'burnley': 4, 'founder': 4, 'theatre': 3, 'hall': 2, 'wwii': 3, 'world war': 3 } found_terms = [] combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() for term, weight in key_terms.items(): if term in combined_text: found_terms.append(term) relevance_score += weight print(f' Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f' Found terms: {", ".join(found_terms[:5])}') # Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'search_index': i, 'result_index': j } search_results['findings'].append(result_data) # Mark high-relevance results as venue candidates if relevance_score >= 8: print(f' üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE - Adding to venue candidates') search_results['venue_candidates'].append(result_data) # Try to extract the webpage content for detailed analysis try: print(f' üìÑ Attempting to fetch webpage content...') headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } page_response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=10) if page_response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(page_response.content, 'html.parser') # Extract text content page_text = soup.get_text() # Save webpage content safe_filename = f'surrey_lodge_search_{i}_{j}_{title[:30].replace(" ", "_").replace("/", "_")}.html' safe_filename = re.sub(r'[^\w\-_\.]', '_', safe_filename) filepath = os.path.join('workspace', safe_filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(page_response.text) print(f' üíæ Saved webpage: {safe_filename}') result_data['saved_file'] = safe_filename # Look for specific historical details in the content historical_indicators = { 'rotating stage': 'rotating stage installation', '1935': 'year 1935 mentioned', 'temperance hall': 'temperance hall reference', 'victorian': 'victorian era connection', 'bomb damage': 'wwii bomb damage', 'burnley': 'burnley relocation', 'founder': 'founder information' } page_text_lower = page_text.lower() historical_findings = [] for indicator, description in historical_indicators.items(): if indicator in page_text_lower: historical_findings.append(description) print(f' ‚úì Found: {description}') result_data['historical_findings'] = historical_findings # Look for birth years and founder names birth_year_pattern = r'\b(18\d{2}|19\d{2})\b' birth_years = re.findall(birth_year_pattern, page_text) if birth_years: print(f' üìÖ Potential birth years found: {", ".join(set(birth_years)[:5])}') result_data['potential_birth_years'] = list(set(birth_years)) # Look for founder names founder_patterns = [ r'founder[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'founded by[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'established by[^.]*?([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)' ] potential_founders = [] for pattern in founder_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) potential_founders.extend(matches) if potential_founders: unique_founders = list(set(potential_founders)) print(f' üë§ Potential founders: {", ".join(unique_founders[:3])}') result_data['potential_founders'] = unique_founders # Add to founder leads for founder in unique_founders: search_results['founder_leads'].append({ 'name': founder, 'source_url': url, 'source_query': query, 'context': 'Surrey Lodge research' }) else: print(f' ‚ùå Failed to fetch webpage (status: {page_response.status_code})') except Exception as e: print(f' ‚ö†Ô∏è Error fetching webpage: {str(e)}') else: print('‚ùå No results found for this query') search_results['search_queries'].append(query) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING SEARCH RESULTS FOR SURREY LODGE IDENTIFICATION') print('=' * 80) total_findings = len(search_results['findings']) print(f'Total search results collected: {total_findings}') print(f'High-relevance venue candidates: {len(search_results["venue_candidates"])}') print(f'Potential founder leads: {len(search_results["founder_leads"])}') if search_results['findings']: # Sort by relevance score search_results['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüìä RELEVANCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) high_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 8] moderate_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 4 <= f['relevance_score'] < 8] print(f'High relevance results (8+ points): {len(high_relevance)}') print(f'Moderate relevance results (4-7 points): {len(moderate_relevance)}') if high_relevance: print('\nüéØ TOP HIGH-RELEVANCE FINDINGS:') for i, finding in enumerate(high_relevance[:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Title: {finding["title"][:80]}...') print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:6])}') if finding.get('historical_findings'): print(f' Historical: {", ".join(finding["historical_findings"][:3])}') if finding.get('potential_founders'): print(f' Founders: {", ".join(finding["potential_founders"][:2])}') if finding.get('potential_birth_years'): print(f' Birth years: {", ".join(finding["potential_birth_years"][:3])}') # Analyze founder leads if search_results['founder_leads']: print('\nüë§ FOUNDER LEADS ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 30) founder_names = [lead['name'] for lead in search_results['founder_leads']] unique_founders = list(set(founder_names)) print(f'Unique potential founders identified: {len(unique_founders)}') for founder in unique_founders[:5]: count = founder_names.count(founder) print(f' ‚Ä¢ {founder} (mentioned {count} time{"s" if count > 1 else ""})') # Create historical timeline from findings timeline_events = [] for finding in search_results['findings']: if finding.get('historical_findings'): for event in finding['historical_findings']: timeline_events.append({ 'event': event, 'source': finding['title'], 'url': finding['url'] }) if timeline_events: print('\nüìÖ HISTORICAL TIMELINE EVENTS IDENTIFIED:') print('-' * 45) unique_events = [] for event in timeline_events: if event['event'] not in [e['event'] for e in unique_events]: unique_events.append(event) for event in unique_events[:8]: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {event["event"]} (from: {event["source"][:50]}...)') search_results['historical_timeline'] = unique_events else: print('‚ùå No search results collected') # Save comprehensive results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'surrey_lodge_comprehensive_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False) UK region for better local results ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') # Process each result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title[:100]}...') print(f' URL: {url}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:150]}...') # Analyze relevance relevance_score = 0 key_terms = { 'surrey lodge': 5, 'south london': 4, 'temperance': 4, 'rotating stage': 5, '1935': 4, 'victorian': 3, 'bomb damage': 4, 'burnley': 4, 'founder': 4, 'theatre': 3, 'hall': 2, 'wwii': 3, 'world war': 3 } found_terms = [] combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() for term, weight in key_terms.items(): if term in combined_text: found_terms.append(term) relevance_score += weight print(f' Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f' Found terms: {", ".join(found_terms[:5])}') # Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'search_index': i, 'result_index': j } search_results['findings'].append(result_data) # import os import json from ddgs import DDGS import time print('=== ANALYZING PREVIOUS SEARCH RESULTS AND CORRECTING SEARCH FOCUS ===') print('Issue identified: Previous search targeted London City Airport instead of Surrey Lodge') print('Correcting search strategy to focus on Surrey Lodge in South London\n') # First, let's examine what files were created in the previous search workspace_files = [f for f in os.listdir('workspace') if f.endswith('.json')] print(f'Found {len(workspace_files)} JSON files in workspace:') for file in workspace_files: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {file}') # Let's inspect the structure of the previous search results to understand the format if workspace_files: sample_file = workspace_files[0] print(f'\nInspecting structure of: {sample_file}') try: with open(os.path.join('workspace', sample_file), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: data = json.load(f) print('File structure:') for key in data.keys(): if isinstance(data[key], list): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(data[key])} items') elif isinstance(data[key], dict): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(data[key])} keys') else: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {type(data[key]).__name__}') except Exception as e: print(f'Error reading file: {str(e)}') print('\n=== CORRECTED SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE SOUTH LONDON ===') print('Objective: Find Surrey Lodge in South London with Victorian temperance hall history') print('Focus: Rotating stage (1935), WWII damage, Burnley relocation, founder birth year\n') # Initialize corrected search results storage search_results = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Find Surrey Lodge South London - Victorian temperance hall with rotating stage', 'search_focus': { 'location': 'Surrey Lodge, South London', 'key_features': ['Victorian temperance hall', 'rotating stage 1935', 'WWII bomb damage', 'Burnley relocation'], 'ultimate_goal': 'Find founder and birth year' }, 'search_queries': [], 'findings': [], 'venue_candidates': [], 'founder_leads': [], 'analysis_summary': {} } # Define corrected search queries specifically for Surrey Lodge corrected_queries = [ '"Surrey Lodge" South London temperance hall Victorian', '"Surrey Lodge" rotating stage 1935 first UK theatre', '"Surrey Lodge" South London World War II bomb damage', '"Surrey Lodge" temperance hall Burnley company relocation', '"Surrey Lodge" South London Victorian founder history', 'Surrey Lodge London temperance movement Victorian era', '"Surrey Lodge" theatre rotating stage 1935 UK first', 'Surrey Lodge South London WWII bombing reconstruction', '"Surrey Lodge" temperance organization founder birth year', 'Surrey Lodge Victorian temperance hall South London history' ] print(f'Executing {len(corrected_queries)} corrected searches for Surrey Lodge:\n') for i, query in enumerate(corrected_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') print('\n=== PHASE 1: CORRECTED WEB SEARCH FOR SURREY LODGE ===') print('=' * 70) # Initialize search engine searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) for i, query in enumerate(corrected_queries, 1): print(f'\nSearch {i}/{len(corrected_queries)}: {query}') print('-' * 60) try: # Perform search with multiple backends and UK region focus results = searcher.text( query, max_results=8, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo", "bing"], safesearch="off", region="en-gb" ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') # Process each result for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') url = result.get('href', 'No URL') snippet = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f'\n Result {j}:') print(f' Title: {title[:80]}...') print(f' URL: {url}') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:120]}...') # Analyze relevance for Surrey Lodge specifically relevance_score = 0 surrey_lodge_terms = { 'surrey lodge': 10, # Highest priority 'temperance hall': 6, 'rotating stage': 8, '1935': 5, 'victorian': 4, 'south london': 5, 'bomb damage': 5, 'burnley': 6, 'founder': 6, 'theatre': 3, 'wwii': 4, 'world war': 4, 'temperance': 5 } found_terms = [] combined_text = f'{title} {snippet}'.lower() for term, weight in surrey_lodge_terms.items(): if term in combined_text: found_terms.append(term) relevance_score += weight print(f' Relevance score: {relevance_score}') print(f' Found terms: {", ".join(found_terms[:4])}') # Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'search_index': i, 'result_index': j } search_results['findings'].append(result_data) # Mark high-relevance results as venue candidates if relevance_score >= 10: # High threshold for Surrey Lodge print(f' üéØ HIGH RELEVANCE - Surrey Lodge candidate!') search_results['venue_candidates'].append(result_data) elif 'surrey lodge' in combined_text: print(f' ‚úì Surrey Lodge mentioned - potential candidate') search_results['venue_candidates'].append(result_data) # Look for founder information founder_keywords = ['founder', 'founded by', 'established by', 'created by'] if any(keyword in combined_text for keyword in founder_keywords): print(f' üë§ Contains founder information') result_data['has_founder_info'] = True else: print('‚ùå No results found for this query') search_results['search_queries'].append(query) # Rate limiting time.sleep(2) except Exception as e: print(f'‚ùå Search error: {str(e)}') time.sleep(3) print('\n' + '=' * 80) print('PHASE 2: ANALYZING CORRECTED SEARCH RESULTS') print('=' * 80) total_findings = len(search_results['findings']) print(f'Total search results collected: {total_findings}') print(f'Surrey Lodge venue candidates: {len(search_results["venue_candidates"])}') if search_results['findings']: # Sort by relevance score search_results['findings'].sort(key=lambda x: x['relevance_score'], reverse=True) print('\nüìä RELEVANCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) high_relevance = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if f['relevance_score'] >= 10] surrey_lodge_mentions = [f for f in search_results['findings'] if 'surrey lodge' in f['title'].lower() or 'surrey lodge' in f['snippet'].lower()] print(f'High relevance results (10+ points): {len(high_relevance)}') print(f'Surrey Lodge mentions: {len(surrey_lodge_mentions)}') if surrey_lodge_mentions: print('\nüéØ SURREY LODGE MENTIONS FOUND:') for i, finding in enumerate(surrey_lodge_mentions[:5], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Title: {finding["title"][:70]}...') print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}') print(f' URL: {finding["url"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:5])}') print(f' Snippet: {finding["snippet"][:100]}...') elif high_relevance: print('\nüîç HIGH RELEVANCE RESULTS (may contain Surrey Lodge info):') for i, finding in enumerate(high_relevance[:3], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Title: {finding["title"][:70]}...') print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:5])}') print(f' Snippet: {finding["snippet"][:100]}...') else: print('\n‚ö†Ô∏è No high-relevance Surrey Lodge results found') print('Showing top results by relevance:') for i, finding in enumerate(search_results['findings'][:3], 1): print(f'\n{i}. Title: {finding["title"][:70]}...') print(f' Score: {finding["relevance_score"]}') print(f' Terms: {", ".join(finding["found_terms"][:4])}') # Analyze all found terms all_terms = [] for finding in search_results['findings']: all_terms.extend(finding['found_terms']) from collections import Counter term_counts = Counter(all_terms) print('\nüìà TERM FREQUENCY ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 30) for term, count in term_counts.most_common(8): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {term}: {count} mentions') # Check for specific Surrey Lodge evidence surrey_lodge_evidence = { 'surrey_lodge_mentioned': any('surrey lodge' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']), 'temperance_hall_found': any('temperance hall' in f['found_terms'] or 'temperance' in f['found_terms'] for f in search_results['findings']), 'founder_info_available': any(f.get('has_founder_info', False) for f in search_results['findings']) } print('\nüîç SURREY LODGE EVIDENCE ANALYSIS:') print('-' * 40) for evidence, found in surrey_lodge_evidence.items(): status = '‚úÖ' if found else '‚ùå' print(f'{status} {evidence.replace("_", " ").title()}: {found}') search_results['analysis_summary']['evidence'] = surrey_lodge_evidence # Calculate confidence level confirmed_count = sum(surrey_lodge_evidence.values()) confidence_percentage = (confirmed_count / len(surrey_lodge_evidence)) * 100 print(f'\nüìà SEARCH CONFIDENCE: {confidence_percentage:.1f}% ({confirmed_count}/{len(surrey_lodge_evidence)} criteria met)') search_results['analysis_summary']['confidence_percentage'] = confidence_percentage else: print('‚ùå No search results collected') # Save corrected search results results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'surrey_lodge_corrected_search.json') with open(results_file, 'w', Store result result_data = { 'query': query, 'title': title, 'url': url, 'snippet': snippet, 'relevance_score': relevance_score, 'found_terms': found_terms, 'search_index': i, 'result_index': j } search_results['findings'].append(result_data) # import os import json import requests from bs4 import BeautifulSoup from ddgs import DDGS import time import re print('=== ANALYZING SURREY LODGE SEARCH RESULTS AND EXTRACTING DETAILED INFORMATION ===') print('Objective: Extract detailed information from identified Surrey Lodge candidates') print('Focus: Emma Cons connection, South London Dwellings Company, and founder details\n') # First, let's examine the corrected search results file to understand what we found results_file = os.path.join('workspace', 'surrey_lodge_corrected_search.json') print('=== PHASE 1: ANALYZING PREVIOUS SEARCH RESULTS ===') print('=' * 60) if os.path.exists(results_file): print(f'Loading search results from: {results_file}') with open(results_file, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f: search_data = json.load(f) print('Search results structure:') for key in search_data.keys(): if isinstance(search_data[key], list): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(search_data[key])} items') elif isinstance(search_data[key], dict): print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {len(search_data[key])} keys') else: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {key}: {type(search_data[key]).__name__}') # Examine venue candidates in detail if 'venue_candidates' in search_data and search_data['venue_candidates']: print(f'\nüéØ VENUE CANDIDATES IDENTIFIED: {len(search_data["venue_candidates"])}') for i, candidate in enumerate(search_data['venue_candidates'], 1): print(f'\nCandidate {i}:') print(f' Title: {candidate.get("title", "Unknown")}') print(f' URL: {candidate.get("url", "Unknown")}') print(f' Relevance: {candidate.get("relevance_score", 0)}') print(f' Terms: {candidate.get("found_terms", [])}') print(f' Snippet: {candidate.get("snippet", "No snippet")[:100]}...') else: print(f'Search results file not found: {results_file}') search_data = {'venue_candidates': []} print('\n=== PHASE 2: DETAILED ANALYSIS OF SURREY LODGE CANDIDATES ===') print('=' * 70) # Initialize detailed analysis results detailed_analysis = { 'timestamp': time.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'), 'objective': 'Extract detailed Surrey Lodge information and founder details', 'candidate_analysis': [], 'founder_information': [], 'historical_timeline': [], 'key_findings': {} } # Key URLs identified from search results key_urls = [ 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emma_Cons', 'https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/South_London_Dwellings_Company', 'https://www.layersoflondon.org/map/records/lambeth-road-surrey-lodge-dwellings-no-124-iris-sylvia-bell' ] print('Analyzing key Surrey Lodge-related URLs:') for i, url in enumerate(key_urls, 1): print(f' {i}. {url}') # Headers for web requests headers = { 'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36' } for i, url in enumerate(key_urls, 1): print(f'\n--- Analyzing URL {i}: {url.split("/")[-1]} ---') try: response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=15) print(f'Status: {response.status_code}') if response.status_code == 200: soup = BeautifulSoup(response.content, 'html.parser') page_text = soup.get_text() # Save the webpage for reference safe_filename = f'surrey_lodge_source_{i}_{url.split("/")[-1].replace("?", "_").replace("=", "_")}.html' filepath = os.path.join('workspace', safe_filename) with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f: f.write(response.text) print(f'Saved webpage: {safe_filename}') # Extract key information analysis = { 'url': url, 'title': soup.find('title').get_text() if soup.find('title') else 'No title', 'saved_file': safe_filename, 'key_findings': [], 'surrey_lodge_mentions': [], 'founder_info': [], 'dates_found': [], 'historical_details': [] } print(f'Page title: {analysis["title"]}') # Look for Surrey Lodge mentions surrey_lodge_pattern = r'[^.]*Surrey Lodge[^.]*\.' surrey_mentions = re.findall(surrey_lodge_pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if surrey_mentions: print(f'Found {len(surrey_mentions)} Surrey Lodge mentions:') for j, mention in enumerate(surrey_mentions[:3], 1): clean_mention = mention.strip() print(f' {j}. {clean_mention[:150]}...') analysis['surrey_lodge_mentions'].append(clean_mention) # Look for founder information founder_patterns = [ r'founded by ([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'established by ([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'created by ([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)', r'([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)[^.]*founded', r'([A-Z][a-z]+ [A-Z][a-z]+)[^.]*established' ] potential_founders = [] for pattern in founder_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) potential_founders.extend(matches) if potential_founders: unique_founders = list(set(potential_founders)) print(f'Potential founders found: {unique_founders[:3]}') analysis['founder_info'] = unique_founders[:5] # Look for birth years and dates date_patterns = [ r'\b(18\d{2})\b', # 1800s dates r'\b(19\d{2})\b', # 1900s dates r'born[^\d]*(18\d{2}|19\d{2})', # Born + year r'birth[^\d]*(18\d{2}|19\d{2})' # Birth + year ] found_dates = [] for pattern in date_patterns: matches = re.findall(pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if isinstance(matches[0], tuple) if matches else False: matches = [match[0] if match[0] else match[1] for match in matches] found_dates.extend(matches) if found_dates: unique_dates = sorted(list(set(found_dates))) print(f'Historical dates found: {unique_dates[:8]}') analysis['dates_found'] = unique_dates # Look for specific historical details historical_keywords = [ 'temperance', 'rotating stage', '1935', 'Victorian', 'bomb damage', 'WWII', 'World War', 'Burnley', 'theatre', 'hall' ] for keyword in historical_keywords: keyword_pattern = f'[^.]*{keyword}[^.]*\.' keyword_mentions = re.findall(keyword_pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if keyword_mentions: print(f'Found {keyword}: {len(keyword_mentions)} mentions') analysis['historical_details'].extend([ {'keyword': keyword, 'context': mention.strip()[:200]} for mention in keyword_mentions[:2] ]) # Special focus on Emma Cons if this is her Wikipedia page if 'Emma_Cons' in url: print('\nüéØ EMMA CONS ANALYSIS:') # Look for birth year specifically emma_birth_pattern = r'Emma Cons[^\(]*\(([^\)]*18\d{2}[^\)]*)') birth_match = re.search(emma_birth_pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if birth_match: birth_info = birth_match.group(1) print(f'Birth information: {birth_info}') analysis['key_findings'].append(f'Emma Cons birth info: {birth_info}') # Look for South London Dwellings Company connection sldc_pattern = r'[^.]*South London Dwellings Company[^.]*\.' sldc_mentions = re.findall(sldc_pattern, page_text, re.IGNORECASE) if sldc_mentions: print(f'South London Dwellings Company mentions: {len(sldc_mentions)}') for mention in sldc_mentions[:2]: print(f' ‚Ä¢ {mention.strip()[:150]}...') analysis['key_findings'].append(f'SLDC connection: {mention.strip()[:200]}') detailed_analysis['candidate_analysis'].append(analysis) else: print(f'Failed to fetch webpage (status: {response.status_code})') except Exception as e: print(f'Error analyzing URL: {str(e)}') time.sleep(2) # Rate limiting print('\n=== PHASE 3: COMPREHENSIVE FOUNDER RESEARCH ===') print('=' * 60) # Based on the analysis, conduct targeted searches for founder information founder_queries = [ '"Emma Cons" born birth year 1838 temperance', '"South London Dwellings Company" founder Emma Cons 1879', 'Emma Cons Surrey Lodge South London Dwellings founder', '"Emma Cons" 1838 birth year Victorian temperance reformer', 'Surrey Lodge Lambeth Emma Cons South London Dwellings Company founder' ] print(f'Conducting {len(founder_queries)} targeted founder searches:') for i, query in enumerate(founder_queries, 1): print(f' {i}. {query}') searcher = DDGS(timeout=15) for i, query in enumerate(founder_queries, 1): print(f'\n--- Founder Search {i}: {query} ---') try: results = searcher.text( query, max_results=5, page=1, backend=["google", "duckduckgo"], safesearch="off", region="en-gb" ) if results: print(f'Found {len(results)} results') for j, result in enumerate(results, 1): title = result.get('title', 'No title') snippet = result.get('body', 'No description') print(f' Result {j}: {title[:60]}...') print(f' Snippet: {snippet[:100]}...') # Look for birth year in snippet birth_year_match = re.search(r'\b(18\d{2})\b', snippet) if birth_year_match: birth_year = birth_year_match.group(1) print(f' üéØ Birth year found: {birth_year}') detailed_analysis['founder_information'].append({ 'query': query, 'source': title, 'birth_year': birth_year, 'context': snippet[:150] }) time.sleep(2) except Exception as e: print(f'Search error: {str(e)}') print('\n=== PHASE 4: CONSOLIDATING FINDINGS ===') print('=' * 50) # Consolidate all findings key_findings = { 'surrey_lodge_identified': False, 'founder_identified': False, 'founder_name': None, 'founder_birth_year': None, 'organization_name': None, 'historical_connections': [], 'confidence_level': 'Low' } # Analyze collected information all_founder_info = [] for analysis in detailed_analysis['candidate_analysis']: all_founder_info.extend(analysis.get('founder_info', [])) for founder_data in detailed_analysis['founder_information']: all_founder_info.append(founder_data.get('source', '')) # Check for Emma Cons as founder if any('Emma Cons' in info for info in all_founder_info): key_findings['founder_identified'] = True key_findings['founder_name'] = 'Emma Cons' key_findings['organization_name'] = 'South London Dwellings Company' #
